##################################################################################[GENERAL SCRIPTED EFFECTS]#################################################################################
#############################################################################################################################################################################################

calculate_b1_b2_for_due_in_h247_event = {
    # This function aims to calculate b1, b2 chances based on FROM (nation to redirect their equipment to Spain) on a number of parameters. The CASE tmp
    # variable refers to the base chances already predetermined. Reminder we will be using __ which takes various sub-b1s/b2s and gets us the arg. In that
    # array we enter the b1 chance.

    ###[Base Chance]###
    if = { limit={ check_variable={ CASE=0 }} set_temp_variable={ base_b1=0 } add_to_temp_array={ tmpCHANCES=0 }}
    else_if = { limit={ check_variable={ CASE=1 }} set_temp_variable={ base_b1=5 } add_to_temp_array={ tmpCHANCES=5 }}
    else_if = { limit={ check_variable={ CASE=2 }} set_temp_variable={ base_b1=15 } add_to_temp_array={ tmpCHANCES=15 }}
    else_if = { limit={ check_variable={ CASE=3 }} set_temp_variable={ base_b1=25 } add_to_temp_array={ tmpCHANCES=25 }}
    else_if = { limit={ check_variable={ CASE=4 }} set_temp_variable={ base_b1=35 } add_to_temp_array={ tmpCHANCES=35 }}
    else_if = { limit={ check_variable={ CASE=5 }} set_temp_variable={ base_b1=45 } add_to_temp_array={ tmpCHANCES=45 }}
    set_temp_variable = { base_b2=100 }
    subtract_from_temp_variable = { base_b2=base_b1 }

    ###[Influence - Only Positive]###
    set_temp_variable={ x=FROM.favor@GRE }
    set_temp_variable={ tmpTHR=0 }
    calculate_linearly_y_ax_b=yes
    set_temp_variable = { ib1=1 }
    subtract_from_temp_variable = { ib1=y }
    multiply_temp_variable = { ib1=100 }
    add_to_temp_array={ tmpCHANCES=ib1 }

    ###[SchactPlan - Only if Germany]###
    if = { 
        limit={ check_variable={ FROM.id=GER.id }}

        set_temp_variable = { schtb1=base_b1 }
        if = { limit={ GRE={ has_idea=GRE_schachtplan }} subtract_from_temp_variable={ schtb1=5 }}
        else_if = { limit={ GRE={ has_idea=GRE_schachtplan_modified }} subtract_from_temp_variable={ schtb1=10 }}
        else_if = { limit={ GRE={ has_idea=GRE_schachtplan_stabilized }} subtract_from_temp_variable={ schtb1=15 }}
        clamp_temp_variable = { var=schtb1 min=0 max=100 }
        add_to_temp_array={ tmpCHANCES=schtb1 }
        log = "scht: [?schtb1]"
    }

    set_temp_variable = { tmpMODE=2 }
    calculate_final_b1_b2_from_temporary_array_tmpCHANCES_with_tmpWEIGHT_and_mode_tmpMODE=yes
}

calculate_b1_b2_for_steal_in_h247_event = {
    # Likewise, we calculate the chance 'stealing' some equipment gets found out.

    ###[Base Chance]###
    if = { limit={ check_variable={ CASE=0 }} set_temp_variable={ base_b1=0 } add_to_temp_array={ tmpCHANCES=0 }}
    else_if = { limit={ check_variable={ CASE=1 }} set_temp_variable={ base_b1=5 } add_to_temp_array={ tmpCHANCES=5 }}
    else_if = { limit={ check_variable={ CASE=2 }} set_temp_variable={ base_b1=15 } add_to_temp_array={ tmpCHANCES=15 }}
    else_if = { limit={ check_variable={ CASE=3 }} set_temp_variable={ base_b1=25 } add_to_temp_array={ tmpCHANCES=25 }}
    else_if = { limit={ check_variable={ CASE=4 }} set_temp_variable={ base_b1=35 } add_to_temp_array={ tmpCHANCES=35 }}
    else_if = { limit={ check_variable={ CASE=5 }} set_temp_variable={ base_b1=45 } add_to_temp_array={ tmpCHANCES=45 }}
    set_temp_variable = { base_b2=100 }
    subtract_from_temp_variable = { base_b2=base_b1 }
    log="Base: b1: [?base_b1], b2: [?base_b2]"

    ###[Agency]### 
    set_temp_variable = { tmpARG1=1 }
    set_temp_variable = { tmpARG2=1 }
    set_temp_variable = { tmpEDIFF=3 }
    calculate_national_intelligence_chance_to_avoid_event=yes

    ###[Civilian/Army/Navy Intelligence]###
    set_temp_variable = { tempTHR=100 }
    add_to_temp_array = { tmpENEMIES=FROM }
    set_temp_variable = { revert_bees=1 }
    calculate_enemy_civilian_intelligence_chance_to_avoid_event=yes
    calculate_enemy_army_intelligence_chance_to_avoid_event=yes
    calculate_enemy_naval_intelligence_chance_to_avoid_event=yes

    ###[Finalize]###
    set_temp_variable = { tmpMODE=0 }                                                           ### We want to take the mean
    add_to_temp_array = { tmpWEIGHT=1.0 }
    add_to_temp_array = { tmpWEIGHT=0.4 }                                                       ### Agency x 1.0, CivINT x 0.4, ArmINT x 0.8, NavINT x 0.6
    add_to_temp_array = { tmpWEIGHT=0.8 }
    add_to_temp_array = { tmpWEIGHT=0.6 }
    calculate_final_b1_b2_from_temporary_array_tmpCHANCES_with_tmpWEIGHT_and_mode_tmpMODE=yes
}

display_base_chances_for_h247_due = {
    # This function aims to display the base_chance for the random list. Sadly, the game cannot precalculate the array runs and showcases 100% 
    # chance although it is fautly.

    effect_tooltip = {
        random_list = {
            base_b1 = { set_variable={ FROM.h247phase=2 tooltip=h247proposal_declined_tt }}
            base_b2 = { set_variable={ FROM.h247phase=1 tooltip=h247proposal_accepted_tt }}
        }
        custom_effect_tooltip=h247_just_average_chances_tt
    }
}

display_actual_chances_for_h247_due = {
    # This function circumverts the issue by showcasing all possible chances. Here it is set that the min b1 chance is selected, so the result
    # is determined beforehand and the player just sees useful information.

    custom_effect_tooltip = h247_rejections_actual_chance_tt
    if = { limit={ check_variable={ FROM.id=GER.id }} custom_effect_tooltip = h247_rejections_actual_chance_schact_tt }
}

display_base_chances_for_h247_steal = {
    # This function aims to display the base_chance for the random list. Sadly, the game cannot precalculate the array runs and showcases 100% 
    # chance although it is fautly.

    effect_tooltip = {
        random_list = {
            base_b1 = { set_variable={ FROM.h247phase=2 tooltip=h247discovered_tt }}
            base_b2 = { set_variable={ FROM.h247phase=1 tooltip=h247notdiscovered_tt }}
        }
        custom_effect_tooltip=h247_just_average_chances_tt
    }
}


display_actual_chances_for_h247_steal = {
    # This function circumverts the issue by showcasing all possible chances. Here it is set that the min b1 chance is selected, so the result
    # is determined beforehand and the player just sees useful information.

    custom_effect_tooltip = h247_rejections_steal_actual_chance_tt
}

########################################################################################
##########################[ AGENCY BONUS/DEBUFF CALCULATORS ]###########################
########################################################################################

calculate_final_b1_b2_from_temporary_array_tmpCHANCES_with_tmpWEIGHT_and_mode_tmpMODE = {
    # This function calculates all distinct b1s & b2s calculated on previous steps to create a final b1, b2 chance for an event. No naming is required, just two arrays in proper order.
    # Chances array contains b1 values and Weight array contains desired weights. Supposedly chances are 50, 75, 80 and our weights are 2, 0.5, 1. Therefore the final outcome will be:
    # 2*50 + 0.5*75 + 1*80 out of 300. 100 + 37.5 + 80 out of 300 => b1 = 217.5/300 = 0.725 which leaves b2 as 0.275. Mode defines function. Mode 0 (default) utilizes weights. Mode 1
    # will take the highest b1 value (and thus lowest b2 value) and Mode 2 will take the lowest of b1 value (and thus highest b2 value).

    ###[Initialization]###
    set_temp_variable = { b1=0 }
    set_temp_variable = { vars_count=tmpCHANCES^num }
    multiply_temp_variable = { vars_count=100 }
    if = { limit={ NOT={ check_variable = { tmpCHANCES^num=tmpWEIGHT^num }}} clear_temp_array=tmpWEIGHT resize_temp_array={ array=tmpWEIGHT value=1 size=tmpCHANCES^num }}
    ###[Refit Weight Array to add up to 1]###
    set_temp_variable = { sum=0 }
    for_each_loop = { array=tmpWEIGHT add_to_temp_variable={ sum=v }}
    for_each_loop = { array=tmpWEIGHT set_temp_variable={ q=v } divide_temp_variable={ q=sum } set_temp_variable={ tmpWEIGHT^i=q }}
    ###[Value*Weight]###
    for_each_loop = {
        array=tmpCHANCES

        set_temp_variable = { tmp=v }
        multiply_temp_variable = { tmp=tmpWEIGHT^i }
        add_to_temp_variable = { b1=tmp }
    }
    ###[Mode]###
    if = {
        limit = { check_variable={ tmpMODE=1 }}
        find_highest_in_array = { array=tmpCHANCES value=b1 }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { check_variable={ tmpMODE=2 }}
        find_lowest_in_array = { array=tmpCHANCES value=b1 }
    }
    set_temp_variable = { b2=100 }
    subtract_from_temp_variable = { b2=b1 }
    log="Final: b1=[?b1|3], b2=[?b2|3]"
}

########################################################################################
##########################[ AGENCY BONUS/DEBUFF CALCULATORS ]###########################
########################################################################################

iterate_calculate_bounded_VAR_chance = {
    # This function essentially matches ARR_VARTOK, ARR_SVIA, ARR_MODE, ARR_tmpLWTHR, ARR_tmpUPTHR, ARR_tmpMAXDIR to the appropriate variables and calls the below functions in a loop. In that way, arrays can be created to make all
    # calculations rather than defying each temp variable again and again. This should be put in a normal for loop in the main bracket, followed either by calculate bounded or enemy bounded var chance.

    set_temp_variable={ VARTOK=ARR_VARTOK^i }
    set_temp_variable={ tmpSVIA=ARR_SVIA^i }
    set_temp_variable={ tmpMODE=ARR_MODE^i }
    set_temp_variable={ tmpLWTHR=ARR_tmpLWTHR^i }
    set_temp_variable={ tmpUPTHR=ARR_tmpUPTHR^i }
    set_temp_variable={ tmpMAXDIR=ARR_tmpMAXDIR^i }
}

calculate_bounded_VAR_chance_to_avoid_event = {
    # REQ: VARTOK, tmpSVIA(opt), tmpMODE(opt), tmpLWTHR(opt), tmpUPTHR(opt), tmpMAXDIR(opt)
    # This function is a group-up of the below functions with boundaries. Works through meta effects, drawing from scripted loc. Variable token (VARTOK) defines which variable to take into consideration. Enemies (tmpENEMIES) contain all the targets
    # to search for. Seek Variable In Allies (tmpSVIA) will additionally search their allies so MODE (tmpMODE) selects either the highest/lowest/mean of variables. VAR_BLOW/BHIGH set the boundaries of the variable depending on VARTOK to avoid bad
    # caps like intel. Subsequently, tmpLWTHR/tmpUPTHR/tmpMAXDIR need to be defined in order to set low/upper thresholds to linearly calculate chances, as well as point which is the maximum direction respectively. For example, 20/40/1 will check
    # between 20-40 linearly (0-1) and match 0 below 20 and 1 above 40. Finally the chances are transformed into proper percentages and b1 (event not happening) is added to the tmpCHANCES array for further calculations if necessary.

    meta_effect={
        text={
            ###[ Initializing ]###
            set_temp_variable={ tmpvarsum=0 }
            THIS = { add_to_temp_array={ tmpFINAL=THIS.id } set_temp_variable={ tmpvar=[VAR] } clamp_temp_variable={ var=tmpvar min=[VAR_BLOW] max=[VAR_BHIGH] } add_to_temp_variable={ tmpvarsum=tmpvar } add_to_temp_array = { tmpVARR=[VAR] }}
            ###[Searching Var Values Amongst Allies]###
            if={
                limit={ check_variable={ tmpSVIA=1 }}

                for_each_scope_loop = {
                    array=tmpENEMIES

                    for_each_scope_loop = {
                        array=allies

                        if = {
                            limit = { NOT={ is_in_array={ array=tmpFINAL value=THIS.id }}}

                            add_to_temp_array = { tmpFINAL=THIS.id }
                            set_temp_variable={ tmpvar=[VAR] } 
                            clamp_temp_variable={ var=tmpvar min=[VAR_BLOW] max=[VAR_BHIGH] } 
                            add_to_temp_variable={ tmpvarsum=tmpvar }
                            add_to_temp_array = { tmpVARR=[VAR] }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            ###[Selection Mode]###
            if = {
                limit = { check_variable={ tmpMODE=1 }}
                find_highest_in_array = { array=tmpVARR value=x index=junk }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = { check_variable={ tmpMODE=2 }}
                find_lowest_in_array = { array=tmpVARR value=x index=junk }
            }
            else = {
                divide_temp_variable={ tmpvarsum=tmpVARR^num }
                set_temp_variable={ x=tmpvarsum }
            }
            log="Calculated Bounded Var Chance (VarName: [VAR])"
        }
        VAR = "[GetVarNameFromVARTOK]"
        VAR_BLOW = "[GetVarUPBOUNDFromVARTOK]"
        VAR_BHIGH = "[GetVarLWBOUNDFromVARTOK]"
    }
    ###[Linear Bounded Calculation]###
    calculate_upper_lower_bounded_y_ax_b=yes
    ###[Transform Back to Percentages]###
    set_temp_variable = { cbv_b2=y }
    multiply_temp_variable = { cbv_b2=100 }
    set_temp_variable = { cbv_b1=100 }
    subtract_from_temp_variable = { cbv_b1=cbv_b2 }
    ###[Clear, Log & Add to Overall Chance Array]###
    clear_temp_array = tmpFINAL
    clear_temp_array = tmpVARR
    log="  b1=[?cbv_b1|2], b2=[?cbv_b2|2]"
    add_to_temp_array = { tmpCHANCES=cbv_b1 }
}

calculate_enemy_bounded_VAR_chance_to_avoid_event = {
    # REQ: VARTOK, tmpENEMIES, tmpSVIA(opt), tmpMODE(opt), tmpLWTHR(opt), tmpUPTHR(opt), tmpMAXDIR(opt)
    # This function is a group-up of the below functions with boundaries. Works through meta effects, drawing from scripted loc. Variable token (VARTOK) defines which variable to take into consideration. Enemies (tmpENEMIES) contain all the targets
    # to search for. Seek Variable In Allies (tmpSVIA) will additionally search their allies so MODE (tmpMODE) selects either the highest/lowest/mean of variables. VAR_BLOW/BHIGH set the boundaries of the variable depending on VARTOK to avoid bad
    # caps like intel. Subsequently, tmpLWTHR/tmpUPTHR/tmpMAXDIR need to be defined in order to set low/upper thresholds to linearly calculate chances, as well as point which is the maximum direction respectively. For example, 20/40/1 will check
    # between 20-40 linearly (0-1) and match 0 below 20 and 1 above 40. Finally the chances are transformed into proper percentages and b1 (event not happening) is added to the tmpCHANCES array for further calculations if necessary.

    meta_effect={
        text={
            ###[ Initializing with tmpENEMIES ]###
            set_temp_variable={ tmpvarsum=0 }
            for_each_scope_loop = { array=tmpENEMIES add_to_temp_array={ tmpFINAL=THIS.id } set_temp_variable={ tmpvar=[VAR] } clamp_temp_variable={ var=tmpvar min=[VAR_BLOW] max=[VAR_BHIGH] } add_to_temp_variable={ tmpvarsum=tmpvar } add_to_temp_array={ tmpVARR=tmpvar }}
            ###[Searching Var Values Amongst Allies]###
            if={
                limit={ check_variable={ tmpSVIA=1 }}

                for_each_scope_loop = {
                    array=tmpENEMIES

                    for_each_scope_loop = {
                        array=allies

                        if = {
                            limit = { NOT={ is_in_array={ array=tmpFINAL value=THIS.id }}}

                            add_to_temp_array = { tmpFINAL=THIS.id }
                            set_temp_variable={ tmpvar=[VAR] } 
                            clamp_temp_variable={ var=tmpvar min=[VAR_BLOW] max=[VAR_BHIGH] } 
                            add_to_temp_variable={ tmpvarsum=tmpvar }
                            add_to_temp_array = { tmpVARR=[VAR] }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            ###[Selection Mode]###
            if = {
                limit = { check_variable={ tmpMODE=1 }}
                find_highest_in_array = { array=tmpVARR value=x index=junk }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = { check_variable={ tmpMODE=2 }}
                find_lowest_in_array = { array=tmpVARR value=x index=junk }
            }
            else = {
                divide_temp_variable={ tmpvarsum=tmpVARR^num }
                set_temp_variable={ x=tmpvarsum }
            }
            log="Calculated Enemy Bounded Var Chance (VarName: [VAR])"
        }
        VAR = "[GetVarNameFromVARTOK]"
        VAR_BLOW = "[GetVarLWBOUNDFromVARTOK]"
        VAR_BHIGH = "[GetVarUPBOUNDFromVARTOK]"
    }
    ###[Linear Bounded Calculation]###
    calculate_upper_lower_bounded_y_ax_b=yes
    ###[Transform Back to Percentages]###
    set_temp_variable = { cebv_b2=y }
    multiply_temp_variable = { cebv_b2=100 }
    set_temp_variable = { cebv_b1=100 }
    subtract_from_temp_variable = { cebv_b1=cebv_b2 }
    ###[Clear, Log & Add to Overall Chance Array]###
    clear_temp_array = tmpFINAL
    clear_temp_array = tmpVARR
    log="  b1=[?cebv_b1|2], b2=[?cebv_b2|2]"
    add_to_temp_array = { tmpCHANCES=cebv_b1 }
}

calculate_enemy_civilian_intelligence_chance_to_avoid_event = {
    # This function calculates the chance to avoid a bad event from certain actions due to low enemy civilian intelligence.

    for_each_scope_loop = { array=tmpENEMIES add_to_temp_array={ tmpFINAL=THIS.id } set_temp_variable={ tmpvar=THIS.civilian_intel@GRE } clamp_temp_variable={ var=tmpvar min=0 max=100 } add_to_temp_array={ tmpARMINT=tmpvar }}
    for_each_scope_loop = {
        array=tmpENEMIES

        for_each_scope_loop = {
            array=allies

            if = {
                limit = { NOT={ is_in_array={ array=tmpFINAL value=THIS.id }}}
                add_to_temp_array = { tmpFINAL=THIS.id }
                add_to_temp_array = { tmpARMINT=THIS.civilian_intel@GRE }
            }
        }
    }
    find_highest_in_array = { array=tmpARMINT value=x index=junk }
    calculate_linearly_y_ax_b=yes
    set_temp_variable = { ccivi_b2=y }
    multiply_temp_variable = { ccivi_b2=100 }
    set_temp_variable = { ccivi_b1=100 }
    subtract_from_temp_variable = { ccivi_b1=ccivi_b2 }
    ############################################
    clear_temp_array = tmpFINAL
    clear_temp_array = tmpARMINT
    if = { limit={ check_variable={ revert_bees=1 }} set_temp_variable={ swp=ccivi_b1 } set_temp_variable={ ccivi_b1=ccivi_b2 } set_temp_variable={ ccivi_b2=swp }}
    log="CIVI: b1=[?ccivi_b1|2], b2=[?ccivi_b2|2]"
    add_to_temp_array = { tmpCHANCES=ccivi_b1 }
}

calculate_enemy_army_intelligence_chance_to_avoid_event = {
    # This function calculates the chance to avoid a bad event from certain actions due to low enemy army intelligence. ENEMIES (tmpENEMIES) is a dynamic array working as following. For each 
    # input, it tries to see if there are any faction members or puppets. If not, then it only runs for that one nation. It eventually takes the maximum possible army intelligence of all 
    # countries in tmpFINAL and linearly calculates two chances like below, depending on tmpTHR.

    for_each_scope_loop = { array=tmpENEMIES add_to_temp_array={ tmpFINAL=THIS.id } set_temp_variable={ tmpvar=THIS.army_intel@GRE } clamp_temp_variable={ var=tmpvar min=0 max=100 } add_to_temp_array={ tmpARMINT=tmpvar }}
    for_each_scope_loop = {
        array=tmpENEMIES

        for_each_scope_loop = {
            array=allies

            if = {
                limit = { NOT={ is_in_array={ array=tmpFINAL value=THIS.id }}}
                add_to_temp_array = { tmpFINAL=THIS.id }
                add_to_temp_array = { tmpARMINT=THIS.army_intel@GRE }
            }
        }
    }
    find_highest_in_array = { array=tmpARMINT value=x index=junk }
    calculate_linearly_y_ax_b=yes
    set_temp_variable = { carmi_b2=y }
    multiply_temp_variable = { carmi_b2=100 }
    set_temp_variable = { carmi_b1=100 }
    subtract_from_temp_variable = { carmi_b1=carmi_b2 }
    ############################################
    clear_temp_array = tmpFINAL
    clear_temp_array = tmpARMINT
    if = { limit={ check_variable={ revert_bees=1 }} set_temp_variable={ swp=carmi_b1 } set_temp_variable={ carmi_b1=carmi_b2 } set_temp_variable={ carmi_b2=swp }}
    log="carmi: b1=[?carmi_b1|2], b2=[?carmi_b2|2]"
    add_to_temp_array = { tmpCHANCES=carmi_b1 }
}

calculate_bounded_world_tension_chance_to_avoid_event = {
    # Req: tmpLWTHR(opt), tmpUPTHR(opt), tmpMAXDIR(opt)
    # This function calculates the chance to avoid a bad event from certain actions due to high world tension. Lower and Upper Threshold specify the range where we apply linear (y=ax+b) calculations.
    # Below/Above min/max values are assigned based off tmpMAXDIR (default: max at upper threshold )

    set_temp_variable = { global_tension=global.threat }
    multiply_temp_variable = { global_tension=100 }
    clamp_temp_variable = { var=global_tension min=0 max=100 }
    set_temp_variable = { x=global_tension }
    calculate_upper_lower_bounded_y_ax_b=yes
    set_temp_variable = { cwt_b2=y }
    multiply_temp_variable = { cwt_b2=100 }
    set_temp_variable = { cwt_b1=100 }
    subtract_from_temp_variable = { cwt_b1=cwt_b2 }
    ############################################
    log="CWT: b1=[?cwt_b1|2], b2=[?cwt_b2|2]"
    add_to_temp_array = { tmpCHANCES=cwt_b1 }
}

calculate_world_tension_chance_to_avoid_event = {
    # This function calculates the chance to avoid a bad event from certain actions due to high world tension. For example, if tmpTHR is 20, then chances are calculated linearly between [0-20) 
    # world tension. If tmpTHR is negative, then the limits are reverted.

    set_temp_variable = { global_tension=global.threat }
    multiply_temp_variable = { global_tension=100 }
    clamp_temp_variable = { var=global_tension min=0 max=100 }
    set_temp_variable = { x=global_tension }
    calculate_linearly_y_ax_b = yes
    set_temp_variable = { cwt_b2=y }
    multiply_temp_variable = { cwt_b2=100 }
    set_temp_variable = { cwt_b1=100 }
    subtract_from_temp_variable = { cwt_b1=cwt_b2 }
    ############################################
    log="CWT: b1=[?cwt_b1|2], b2=[?cwt_b2|2]"
    add_to_temp_array = { tmpCHANCES=cwt_b1 }
}

calculate_national_intelligence_chance_to_avoid_event = {
    # This function calculates your national ability to avoid bad events from certain actions. Takes as input tmpEDIFF (event difficulty). Arguments tmpARG1, tmpARG2 are magnitude
    # adjusters on the two main parameters that define success (default=1). (Maxes with 1 arg: About 10 Counter Int, 31 agency upgrades )
    # RETURNS: cni_b1, cni_b2 (chances for random list)
    
    if = { limit={ has_intelligence_agency=no } set_temp_variable={ base=-100 }}
    else = {
        set_temp_variable = { base=modifier@intelligence_agency_defense }
        multiply_temp_variable = { base=tmpARG1?1 }
        set_temp_variable = { bonus=GRE.agency_upgrade_number }
        multiply_temp_variable = { bonus=tmpARG2?1 }
        add_to_temp_variable = { base=bonus }
    }
    set_temp_variable = { divider=base }
    add_to_temp_variable = { divider=tmpEDIFF }
    set_temp_variable = { cni_b1=base }
    divide_temp_variable = { cni_b1=divider }
    multiply_temp_variable = { cni_b1=100 }
    set_temp_variable = { cni_b2=100 }
    subtract_from_temp_variable = { cni_b2=cni_b1 }
    ############################################
    log="CNI: b1=[?cni_b1|2], b2=[?cni_b2|2]"
    add_to_temp_array = { tmpCHANCES=cni_b1 }
}

calculate_THIS_debt_difference_chance_to_avoid_event = {
    # This function calculates the chance to avoid a protest event from the other two parties, in case the current one has been paid while having at least tmpTHR. The chance linearly increases at it reaches its maximum (100-tmpTHR).
    # ScaleMAG is an optional argument that will scale tmpMAG variable depending on the difference. cred_paid is the creditor paid, while THIS is potential protester.

    set_temp_variable = { cur_debt=GRE.debt@var:cred_paid }
    set_temp_variable = { debt_diff=GRE.debt@THIS }
    subtract_from_temp_variable = { debt_diff=cur_debt }
    
    if = {
        limit = { check_variable={ tmpSCALEMAG=1 }}
        set_temp_variable = { tmpMAG=debt_diff }
        divide_temp_variable = { tmpMAG=5 }
    }
    log = "CD: [?GRE.debt@var:cred_paid], DD: [?GRE.debt@THIS], DIFF: [?debt_diff], TMAG: [?tmpMAG]"
    if = {
        limit = { check_variable={ debt_diff>10 }}
        set_temp_variable = { tmpTHR=GRE.debt@THIS }
        set_temp_variable = { x=GRE.debt@var:cred_paid }
        calculate_linearly_y_ax_b=yes
        set_temp_variable = { tdf_b2=y }
        multiply_temp_variable = { tdf_b2=100 }
        #divide_temp_variable = { tdf_b2=4 }                     # This division here aims to lower the % of proc, because you essentially spam this every time you pay something.
        set_temp_variable = { tdf_b1=100 }
        subtract_from_temp_variable = { tdf_b1=tdf_b2 }
    }
    else = {
        set_temp_variable = { tdf_b1=100 }
        set_temp_variable = { tdf_b2=0 }
    }
    add_to_temp_array = { tmpCHANCES=tdf_b1 }
    log="TDF: b1=[?tdf_b1|2], b2=[?tdf_b2|2]"
}

calculate_linearly_y_ax_b = {
    # This function calculates y=ax+b as we did in highschool due to the game's and my personal limitations to reach up to this point. If tmpTHR is positive, then it considers 0 the max 
    # to give a weight of 1, otherwise if tmpTHR is negative, this gets reverted to consider 1 as the maximum point. In other words, if thr=20, then we check between [0, 20], if thr=-20,
    # we check between [20, 100]. Takes X as input (e.g. world tension) and tmpTHR. tmpREV reverses in which limit max resides. Returns y

    if = {                                                                      # (cwt_b2 = x * -1/tmpTHR + 1)
        limit = { check_variable={ tmpTHR>0 }}
        clamp_temp_variable = { var=x max=tmpTHR }
        multiply_temp_variable = { x=-1 }
        divide_temp_variable = { x=tmpTHR }
        set_temp_variable = { y=1 }
        add_to_temp_variable = { y=x }
        if={ limit={ check_variable={ tmpREV=1 }} set_temp_variable={ swp=1 } subtract_from_temp_variable={ swp=y } set_temp_variable={ y=swp }}
    }
    else = {                                                                    # (cwt_b2 = (x-tmpTHR)/(100-tmpTHR))
        multiply_temp_variable = { tmpTHR=-1 }
        clamp_temp_variable = { var=x min=tmpTHR }
        subtract_from_temp_variable = { x=tmpTHR }
        set_temp_variable = { divider=100 }
        subtract_from_temp_variable = { divider=tmpTHR }
        divide_temp_variable = { x=divider }
        set_temp_variable = { y=x }
        if={ limit={ check_variable={ tmpREV=1 }} set_temp_variable={ swp=1 } subtract_from_temp_variable={ swp=y } set_temp_variable={ y=swp }}
    }
}

calculate_upper_lower_bounded_y_ax_b = {
    # The following function essentially covers cases where we desire a certain upper/lower limit. For example, we may need max values after 50, or min values below 20. In that regard we define
    # two extra areas were we match max/min and in-between we essentially apply calculate_linearly_y_ax_b but with upper and lower limits. tmpUPTHR, tmpLTHR are upper/lower thresholds respectively
    # and tmpMAXDIR the direction of MAX (1). 0 implies max is in tmpLWTHR, 1 in tmpUPTHR. Defaults to 0/100/1.

    if={
        limit={ check_variable={ var=x value=tmpLWTHR?0 compare=less_than_or_equals }}
        if={ limit={ check_variable={ tmpMAXDIR?1=0 }} set_temp_variable={ y=1 }}
        else={ set_temp_variable={ y=0 }}
    }
    else_if={
        limit={ check_variable={ var=x value=tmpUPTHR?100 compare=greater_than_or_equals }}
        if={ limit={ check_variable={ tmpMAXDIR?1=0 }} set_temp_variable={ y=0 }}
        else={ set_temp_variable={ y=1 }}
    }
    else={                                                                    # y = (x-tmpLWTHR)/(tmpUPTHR-tmpLWTHR)
        set_temp_variable={ y=x }
        subtract_from_temp_variable={ y=tmpLWTHR }
        set_temp_variable={ divider=tmpUPTHR?100 }
        subtract_from_temp_variable={ divider=tmpLWTHR }
        divide_temp_variable={ y=divider }
        if={ limit={ check_variable={ tmpMAXDIR?1=0 }} set_temp_variable={ swp=1 } subtract_from_temp_variable={ swp=y } set_temp_variable={ y=swp }}
    }
}

vscope_add_set_character_mbranch = {
    # This function utilizes v scope to detect and subsequently add/set character military branch to array/variable.

    if={ limit={ OR={ is_army_leader=yes is_corps_commander=yes has_army_ledger=yes is_character_slot=army_chief }} add_to_array={ GRE.c_mbranch@1=var:v } set_variable={ GRE.c_mbranch@var:v=1 }}
    if={ limit={ OR={ is_navy_leader=yes has_navy_ledger=yes is_character_slot=navy_chief }}                        add_to_array={ GRE.c_mbranch@2=var:v } set_variable={ GRE.c_mbranch@var:v=2 }}
    if={ limit={ OR={ has_air_ledger=yes is_character_slot=air_chief }}                                            add_to_array={ GRE.c_mbranch@3=var:v } set_variable={ GRE.c_mbranch@var:v=3 }}
}

vscope_add_set_character_ideology = {
    # This function utilizes v scope to detect and subsequently add/set character ideology to array/variable.

	if = { limit = { has_trait=trait_GRE_stauch_monarchist_persona } 		add_to_array={ GRE.c_ideology@1=var:v } set_variable={ GRE.c_ideology@var:v=1 }}
	else_if = { limit = { has_trait=trait_GRE_stauch_republican_persona } 	add_to_array={ GRE.c_ideology@2=var:v } set_variable={ GRE.c_ideology@var:v=2 }}
	else_if = { limit = { has_trait=trait_GRE_stauch_communist_persona } 	add_to_array={ GRE.c_ideology@3=var:v } set_variable={ GRE.c_ideology@var:v=3 }}
	else_if = { limit = { has_trait=trait_GRE_stauch_fascist_persona } 		add_to_array={ GRE.c_ideology@4=var:v } set_variable={ GRE.c_ideology@var:v=4 }}
	else_if = { limit = { has_trait=trait_GRE_conventional_leanings } 		add_to_array={ GRE.c_ideology@5=var:v } set_variable={ GRE.c_ideology@var:v=5 }}
	else_if = { limit = { has_trait=trait_GRE_socialdemocratic_leanings } 	add_to_array={ GRE.c_ideology@6=var:v } set_variable={ GRE.c_ideology@var:v=6 }}
	else_if = { limit = { has_trait=trait_GRE_revolutionary_leanings } 		add_to_array={ GRE.c_ideology@7=var:v } set_variable={ GRE.c_ideology@var:v=7 }}
	else_if = { limit = { has_trait=trait_GRE_monarchofascism_leanings } 	add_to_array={ GRE.c_ideology@8=var:v } set_variable={ GRE.c_ideology@var:v=8 }}
}

calculate_bodosakis_experience_for_upgrade={
    # Simple function utilizing mod to keep increasing Bodosakis' trait.

    set_temp_variable={ lvl=GRE.bodosakis_experience }
    effect_tooltip={ increase_bodosakis_trait=yes }
    hidden_effect={
        if={
            limit={ check_variable={ var=lvl value=100 compare=greater_than_or_equals }}
            modulo_temp_variable={ lvl=100 }
            set_variable={ GRE.bodosakis_experience=lvl }
            increase_bodosakis_trait=yes
        }
    }
}

increase_eon_spirit_through_kanellopoulos = {
    if = {
        limit = { has_idea=GRE_eon }
        swap_ideas = { remove_idea=GRE_eon add_idea=GRE_eon_kanellopoulos_year_1 }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { has_idea=GRE_eon_kanellopoulos_year_1 }
        swap_ideas = { remove_idea=GRE_eon_kanellopoulos_year_1 add_idea=GRE_eon_kanellopoulos_year_2 }
    }
}

increase_bodosakis_trait = {
    if = {
        limit = { check_variable={ pa_rank@var:bodosakis<7 }}

        set_temp_variable={ crank=pa_rank@var:bodosakis }
        add_to_variable={ pa_rank@var:bodosakis=1 }
        set_temp_variable={ nrank=pa_rank@var:bodosakis }
        custom_effect_tooltip = bodosakis_seicho_tt
        hidden_effect = {
            meta_effect = {
                text = {
                    remove_trait = {
                        character = GRE_prodromos_bodosakis
                        slot = political_advisor
                        trait = business_genius_[CLVL]
                    }
                    add_trait = {
                        character = GRE_prodromos_bodosakis
                        slot = political_advisor
                        trait = business_genius_[NLVL]
                    }
                }
                CLVL = "[?crank]"
                NLVL = "[?nrank]"
            }
        }
    }
}

calculate_schachtplan_decision_costs = { 
    # This function calculates the cost of Schachtplan decision based on certain parameters.
    
    set_temp_variable={ cur_cost=GRE.schachtplan_actual_cost }
    #####[ Calculate Display Cost and Reductions on Current Cost ]#####
    set_temp_variable={ bonus_off=1 }
    if = { limit={ any_operative_leader={ operative_leader_mission=diplomatic_pressure check_variable={ operation_country = GER:id }} subtract_from_temp_variable={ bonus_off=0.2 }}}
    if = { limit={ any_operative_leader={ operative_leader_mission=control_trade check_variable={ operation_country = GER:id }} subtract_from_temp_variable={ bonus_off=0.1 }}}
    multiply_temp_variable={ cur_cost=bonus_off }
    set_variable={ GRE.schachtplan_cost=cur_cost }
}

calculate_investment_decision_cost_tmpC_FROM = {
    # This function calculates the cost of Investment Decisions likewise. Only to be used inside decision where FROM is target country.

    set_temp_variable={ cur_cost=tmpC }
    #####[ Calculate Display Cost and Reductions on Current Cost ]#####
    set_temp_variable={ bonus_off=1 }
    if = { limit={ any_operative_leader={ operative_leader_mission=diplomatic_pressure check_variable={ operation_country = FROM:id }} subtract_from_temp_variable={ bonus_off=0.2 }}}
    if = { limit={ any_operative_leader={ operative_leader_mission=control_trade check_variable={ operation_country = FROM:id }} subtract_from_temp_variable={ bonus_off=0.1 }}}
    multiply_temp_variable={ cur_cost=bonus_off }
}

expand_greek_railway_system_generator ={
    # As in python, this generator retains state and upgrades the railway system accordingly.

    custom_effect_tooltip = railway_system_expansion_level_tt
    if = {
        limit = { check_variable={ GRE.railway_expansion_level=0 }}
        custom_effect_tooltip = railway_system_expansion_0_tt
        hidden_effect = {
            build_railway = { start_state=47 target_state=913 }
            build_railway = { path = { 4109 1109 3988 7211 } }
            build_railway = { path = { 11818 3936 6990 9930 13263 11774 11905 } }
            build_railway = { path = { 11895 3844 3864 } }
            909 = {
                add_building_construction = {
                    type = naval_base
                    level = 1
                    instant_build = yes
                    province = 13272
                }
            }
            build_railway = {
                path = { 13272 12001 }
            }
            hidden_effect = {
                build_railway = { path = { 11895 13269 } }
                build_railway = { path = { 3988 7096 } }
            }
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { check_variable={ GRE.railway_expansion_level=1 }}
        custom_effect_tooltip = railway_system_expansion_1_tt
        hidden_effect = {
            47 = {
                add_building_construction = {
                    type = infrastructure
                    level = 1
                    instant_build = yes
                }
            }
            913 = {
                add_building_construction = {
                    type = infrastructure
                    level = 1
                    instant_build = yes
                }
            }

            build_railway = { path = { 11818 3936 6990 9930 13263 11774 11905 } }
            build_railway = { path = { 7211 4193 1173 4178 4078 7096 } }
        }
    }
    else_if = { 
        limit = { check_variable={ GRE.railway_expansion_level=2 }}
        custom_effect_tooltip = railway_system_expansion_2_tt
        hidden_effect = {
            185 = { add_building_construction = { type=infrastructure level=1 instant_build=yes }}

        }
    }
    else_if = { 
        limit = { check_variable={ GRE.railway_expansion_level=3 }}
        custom_effect_tooltip = railway_system_expansion_3_tt
        hidden_effect = {
            910 = { add_building_construction = { type=fuel_silo level=1 instant_build=yes }}

            914 = { add_building_construction = { type=supply_node province=9930 level=1 instant_build=yes }}
            build_railway = { path = { 13269 13273 9916 } }
            build_railway = { path = { 3914 9805 } }
        }
    }
    else_if = { 
        limit = { check_variable={ GRE.railway_expansion_level=4 }}
        custom_effect_tooltip = railway_system_expansion_4_tt
        hidden_effect = {
            910 = { add_building_construction = { type=fuel_silo level=1 instant_build=yes }}
            186 = { add_building_construction = { type=fuel_silo level=1 instant_build=yes }}
            47 = { add_building_construction = { type=infrastructure level=1 instant_build=yes }}
            913 = { add_building_construction = { type=infrastructure level=1 instant_build=yes }}
            186 = { add_building_construction = { type=infrastructure level=1 instant_build=yes }}
            909 = { add_building_construction = { type=infrastructure level=1 instant_build=yes }}
            185 = { add_building_construction = { type=infrastructure level=1 instant_build=yes }}
            912 = { add_building_construction = { type=infrastructure level=1 instant_build=yes }}
            910 = { add_building_construction = { type=infrastructure level=1 instant_build=yes }}
            every_controlled_state = { 
                if = {
                    limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_inaccessible_region } }
                    remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_inaccessible_region }
                }
            }
        }
    }
    add_to_variable = { GRE.railway_expansion_level=1 }
}

set_linear_influence_weights_with_THIS = {
    # This function lineary sets bonuses/nerfs depending on influence. (y = 0.01x)

    set_temp_variable = { wght=0.01 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { wght=THIS.favor@GRE }
}

set_linear_parameter_thisPAR_weights = {
    # This function lineary sets weights depending on parameter thisPAR (temp_var), with max/min values parMAX, parMIN. Best outcome will always be 1.
    # NEG: y = -thisPAR/parMIN
    # POS: y = thisPAR/parMAX

    set_temp_variable = { par_wght=thisPAR }
    if = { limit={ check_variable={ thisPAR>0 }} divide_temp_variable = { par_wght=parMAX } }
    else = { divide_temp_variable = { par_wght=parMIN } }
}

calculate_potential_reductor_tmpIMP_outside = {
    # This function aims to limit certain report events due to expanding the influence mechanic on all nations (from a subset).

    set_temp_variable={ base_b1=b1 } 
    set_temp_variable={ base_b2=b2 }
    set_temp_variable={ reductor=tmpIMP?1 }
}

calculate_potential_reductor_tmpIMP_inside = {
    # This function aims to limit certain report events due to expanding the influence mechanic on all nations (from a subset).

    set_temp_variable = { b1=base_b1 }
    set_temp_variable = { b2=base_b2 }
    if = {
        limit = { NOT={ is_in_array={ array=GRE.important_nations value=THIS.id }}}

        set_temp_variable = { reductor=tmpIMP?1 }
        multiply_temp_variable={ b2=reductor } 
        set_temp_variable={ b1=100 } 
        subtract_from_temp_variable={ b1=b2 }
    }
}

potentially_send_report_events_for_action_tmpREAC1_with_args_tmpARRVAL_tmpMAG_and_code = {
    # This function determines whether positive/negative events will be fired by nations when you activate x decisions. Decisions are in X code (meaning you need 
    # to insert only ONE codes, like 51 for industrial expansion. Code is XXXX form, depicting Mon/Dem/Com/Fas. 0 depicts no results, 1 depicts favorable/negative 
    # results depending on the code selected. ARRVAL is an optional temp array storing all values which depend on feature set. For example, if I set 
    # 60/61 which is for authoritarian actions, tmpARRVAL has to include favor won/lost (2 vars). MAG is for magnitude (default(mostly)/user choices x times).

    calculate_potential_reductor_tmpIMP_outside=yes
    for_each_scope_loop = {
        array = global.favor_mechanic

        if = { limit={ check_variable={ reductor<1 }} calculate_potential_reductor_tmpIMP_inside=yes }
        random_list = {
            seed=random
            #log=yes
            b1 = { }
            b2 = {
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        OR = {
                            AND = { has_government=neutrality check_variable={ CM=1 } }
                            AND = { has_government=democratic check_variable={ CD=1 } }
                            AND = { has_government=communism check_variable={ CC=1 } }
                            AND = { has_government=fascism check_variable={ CF=1 } }
                        }
                    }
                    set_variable = { THIS.init_e332t@GRE=tmpREAC1 }
                    set_variable = { THIS.init_e332MAG@GRE=tmpMAG }
                    set_temp_variable_to_random = { var=tmpX min=0 max=7 integer=yes }
                    set_variable = { THIS.init_e332d@GRE=tmpX }
                    country_event = { id = hellas.3331 days=1 }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

potentially_send_report_events_for_actions_tmpREAC1_tmpREAC2_with_args_tmpARRVAL_tmpMAG_and_code = {
    # This function determines whether positive/negative events will be fired by nations when you activate xx decisions. Decisions are in XX code (meaning you need 
    # to insert a combination of codes, like 60 and 61 for authoritarian. Code is XXXX form, depicting Mon/Dem/Com/Fas (CM/CD/CC/CF). 0 depicts no results, 1 depicts 
    # favorable results, whereas 2 depicts negative results. ARRVAL is an optional temp array storing all values which depend on feature set. For example, if I set 
    # 60/61 which is for authoritarian actions, tmpARRVAL has to include favor won/lost (2 vars). MAG is for magnitude (default(mostly)/user choices x times).
    # tmpIMP [0, 1] is the percentage of chance reduction for an event to happen on NON important nations. Defaults to 1 (equal chance)

    calculate_potential_reductor_tmpIMP_outside=yes
    for_each_scope_loop = {
        array = global.favor_mechanic

        if = { limit={ check_variable={ reductor<1 }} calculate_potential_reductor_tmpIMP_inside=yes }
        if = { limit = { check_variable={ THIS=GER.id }} log = "Ab1: [?b1], Ab2: [?b2]" }
        if = { limit = { check_variable={ THIS=VEN.id }} log = "Ab1: [?b1], Ab2: [?b2]" }
        random_list = {
            seed=random
            #log=yes
            b1 = { }
            b2 = {
                for_each_loop = { array=tmpARRVAL add_to_array={THIS.init_e332ARRVAL@GRE=v }}
                set_variable = { THIS.init_e332MAG@GRE=tmpMAG }
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        OR = {
                            AND = { has_government=neutrality check_variable={ CM=1 } }
                            AND = { has_government=democratic check_variable={ CD=1 } }
                            AND = { has_government=communism check_variable={ CC=1 } }
                            AND = { has_government=fascism check_variable={ CF=1 } }
                        }
                    }
                    set_variable = { THIS.init_e332t@GRE=tmpREAC1 }
                    set_temp_variable_to_random = { var=tmpX min=0 max=7 integer=yes }
                    set_variable = { THIS.init_e332d@GRE=tmpX }
                    country_event = { id = hellas.3331 days=1 }
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        OR = {
                            AND = { has_government=neutrality check_variable={ CM=2 } }
                            AND = { has_government=democratic check_variable={ CD=2 } }
                            AND = { has_government=communism check_variable={ CC=2 } }
                            AND = { has_government=fascism check_variable={ CF=2 } }
                        }
                    }
                    set_variable = { THIS.init_e332t@GRE=tmpREAC2 }
                    set_temp_variable_to_random = { var=tmpX min=0 max=7 integer=yes }
                    set_variable = { THIS.init_e332d@GRE=tmpX }
                    country_event = { id = hellas.3331 days=1 }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

potentially_send_report_events_for_action_tmpREAC1_with_args_tmpARRVAL_tmpMAG_to_targets_tmpRECEIVERS = {
    # This function determines whether positive/negative events will be fired by nations when you activate x decisions. Decisions are in X code (meaning you need 
    # to insert only ONE codes, like 51 for industrial expansion. Receivers are a temp array of nations that a report event will be judged for.
    
    calculate_potential_reductor_tmpIMP_outside=yes
    for_each_scope_loop = {
        array = tmpRECEIVERS

        if = { limit={ check_variable={ reductor<1 }} calculate_potential_reductor_tmpIMP_inside=yes }
        random_list = {
            seed=random
            log=yes
            b1 = { }
            b2 = {
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        check_variable = { tmpREAC1=52 }
                        mussolini_historical_tensions_with_greece = yes
                    }
                    set_variable = { THIS.init_e332t@GRE=tmpREAC1 }
                    set_variable = { THIS.init_e332MAG@GRE=tmpMAG }
                    set_temp_variable_to_random = { var=tmpX min=0 max=7 integer=yes }
                    set_variable = { THIS.init_e332d@GRE=tmpX }
                    country_event = { id = hellas.3331 days=1 }
                }
                else = {
                    set_variable = { THIS.init_e332t@GRE=tmpREAC1 }
                    set_variable = { THIS.init_e332MAG@GRE=tmpMAG }
                    set_temp_variable_to_random = { var=tmpX min=0 max=7 integer=yes }
                    set_variable = { THIS.init_e332d@GRE=tmpX }
                    country_event = { id = hellas.3331 days=1 }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

potentially_send_report_events_for_unevently_paid_debt_gui = {
    # This function calculates whether player paid more debt towards one nation over the other, in which case a diplomatic protest will take place.

    set_temp_variable = { index=1 }
    add_to_temp_array = { debt_collectors=ENG.id }
    add_to_temp_array = { debt_collectors=FRA.id }
    add_to_temp_array = { debt_collectors=ITA.id }
    for_each_scope_loop = {
        array = debt_collectors

        if={
            limit={
                NOT={ check_variable = { THIS=GRE.ecall_selector }}
                set_temp_variable = { x=GRE.debt@THIS }
                subtract_from_temp_variable = { x=GRE.debt@var:GRE.ecall_selector }
                check_variable = { var=x value=15 compare=greater_than_or_equals}
            }
            set_linear_influence_weights_with_THIS=yes
            multiply_temp_variable = { wght=25 }
            set_temp_variable = { tmp=x }
            subtract_from_temp_variable = { tmp=15 }
            divide_temp_variable = { tmp=5 }
            set_temp_variable = { wght2=-2 }
            multiply_temp_variable = { wght2=tmp }
            set_temp_variable = { b1=50 }
            set_temp_variable = { b2=50 }
            add_to_temp_variable = { b1=wght }
            add_to_temp_variable = { b1=wght }
            subtract_from_temp_variable = { b2=wght }
            subtract_from_temp_variable = { b2=wght }
            random_list = {
                seed=random
                b1 = { }
                b2 = { set_variable = { THIS.init_e332t@GRE=50 } set_variable = { THIS.init_e332d@GRE=1 } country_event = { id = hellas.3331 days=1 }  }
            }
        }
    }
}

potentially_send_report_events_for_unevently_paid_debt = {
    # This function calculates whether player paid more debt towards one nation over the other, in which case a diplomatic protest will take place.

    set_temp_variable = { index=1 }
    add_to_temp_array = { debt_collectors=ENG.id }
    add_to_temp_array = { debt_collectors=FRA.id }
    add_to_temp_array = { debt_collectors=ITA.id }
    for_each_scope_loop = {
        array = debt_collectors

        if={
            limit={
                NOT={ check_variable = { THIS.id=PREV.FROM.id }}
                set_temp_variable = { x=GRE.debt@THIS }
                subtract_from_temp_variable = { x=GRE.debt@PREV.FROM }
                check_variable = { var=x value=15 compare=greater_than_or_equals}
            }
            set_linear_influence_weights_with_THIS=yes
            multiply_temp_variable = { wght=25 }
            set_temp_variable = { tmp=x }
            subtract_from_temp_variable = { tmp=15 }
            divide_temp_variable = { tmp=5 }
            set_temp_variable = { wght2=-2 }
            multiply_temp_variable = { wght2=tmp }
            set_temp_variable = { b1=50 }
            set_temp_variable = { b2=50 }
            add_to_temp_variable = { b1=wght }
            add_to_temp_variable = { b1=wght }
            subtract_from_temp_variable = { b2=wght }
            subtract_from_temp_variable = { b2=wght }
            random_list = {
                seed=random
                b1 = { }
                b2 = { set_variable = { THIS.init_e332t@GRE=50 } set_variable = { THIS.init_e332d@GRE=1 } country_event = { id = hellas.3331 days=1 }  }
            }
        }
    }
}

send_event_FROM_scope_to_GRE_of_type_tmpT_in_days_tmpD = {
    # This function works as a stack for event senders. We send through an event because its mandatory if we want FROM to depict sender nation (otherwise we get our nation) back which breaks everything.
    # We have no problem when same id is used by different scopes (GER+ITA) but we have a problem when we want to send an event by nation X 7 days later while event another of nation X is to be sent 
    # after 3 days. In that case we would override the variables. In that regard we keep a stack of 7 events. The only case we have an error is when a nation is to send more than 7 report events
    # in a few days in that case events will be lost.
    
    #log="Scope is: [?THIS.GetName]"
    #log="T: [?THIS.init_e332t@GRE], D: [?THIS.init_e332d@GRE]"

    set_temp_variable = { event_index=1 }
    resize_temp_array = { array=stack value=1 size=7 }
    for_each_loop = {
        array = stack

        #log="THIS; [THIS.GetName]"
        meta_effect = {
            text = {
                if = {
                    limit = { NOT={ is_in_array={ array=GRE.e_332_[STACK_POS] value=THIS.id }}}
                    add_to_array = { GRE.e_332_[STACK_POS]=THIS.id }
                    set_variable = { THIS.e332_[STACK_POS]_t@GRE=THIS.init_e332t@GRE }
                    set_variable = { THIS.e332_[STACK_POS]_MAG@GRE=THIS.init_e332MAG@GRE }
                    for_each_loop = { array=THIS.init_e332ARRVAL@GRE add_to_array={THIS.e332_[STACK_POS]_ARRVAL@GRE=v }}
                    GRE = { country_event={ id=hellas.332000[STACK_POS] days=PREV.init_e332d@GRE }}
                    set_temp_variable={ break=1 }
                }
            }
            STACK_POS = "[?event_index|.0]"
        }
        add_to_temp_variable = { event_index=1 }
    }
    clear_variable = THIS.init_e332t@GRE
    clear_variable = THIS.init_e332d@GRE
}


########################################################################################
######################[ Gold Reserves from Armament Transaction ]#######################
########################################################################################

recalculate_gold_reserve_bonuses = {
    # Recalculates pp bonus from base token worth.

    set_temp_variable = { btw=0.10 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { btw=GRE.gold_reserves }
    set_variable = { gre_arms_deal_pp=btw }
    clamp_variable={ var=gre_arms_deal_pp min=0 max=1 }
}

########################################################################################
##############################[ DEBT TO THE IFC REVAMPED ]##############################
########################################################################################

#GRE_update_debt_status
#GRE_calculate_effects_of_debt
#GRE_debt_flags_check

GRE_update_debt_status = {                                                   ### Updates debt status for all three nations (ENG/FRA/ITA) and total debt paid. Enters through country scope!
    subtract_from_variable = { GRE.debt@THIS = GRE.debt_package }             ## Subtract from scope's stack the debt package (defined by decision, either small or big)
    add_to_variable = { GRE.paid_debt@THIS = GRE.debt_package }               ## Keep count of how much debt Greece paid to THIS (gui purposes).
    add_to_variable = { GRE.GRE_debt_to_the_ifc_paid_var = GRE.debt_package } ## Add package to total counter 
    set_variable = { GRE.debt_package = 0 }                                   ## Resets the package to 0
    GRE = { GRE_calculate_effects_of_debt = yes }                             ## Calls below scripted effect through the scope of Greece
}

GRE_calculate_effects_of_debt = {                                            ### Formula: For 0 debt payed, -25% stability, -20% consumer goods. Stability degrades slower, consumer goods faster. Pivotal is the 0-50% paid range
    set_temp_variable = { x = 300 }
    subtract_from_temp_variable = { x = GRE_debt_to_the_ifc_paid_var }       ## We subtract what we've payed.
    if = { 
        limit = {
            check_variable = { x > 150 }                                     ## means we've payed less than half total debt.
        }                                                                     # y = -0.001x + 0.05 , y = -0.001x + 0.1 
        multiply_temp_variable = { x = -0.001 }
        set_temp_variable = { y = x }
        add_to_temp_variable = { x = 0.05 }
        add_to_temp_variable = { y = 0.10 }
        set_variable = { debt_to_the_ifc_stb = x }
        multiply_temp_variable = { y = -1 }
        set_variable = { debt_to_the_ifc_cons = y }
    }
    else = {                                                                  # y = 0,000666666667, y = 0,000333333333 - 0.2 ||| Nicely it seems that cons = 1/2 stb so we take advantage to simplify code
        multiply_temp_variable = { x = -0.667 }
        set_variable = { xx = x }
        divide_temp_variable = { x = 1000 }
        set_variable = { debt_to_the_ifc_stb = x }
        divide_temp_variable = { x = -2 }
        set_variable = { debt_to_the_ifc_cons = x }
    }
    set_temp_variable = { y = GRE_debt_to_the_ifc_paid_var }                 ## Here we calculate % of debt paid to print into the category
    divide_temp_variable = { y = 3 }
    set_variable = { GRE_debt_to_the_ifc_paid_var_cat = y }
    GRE_debt_flags_check = yes                                               ## Final jump, we set flags if any debt was fully paid
}

GRE_debt_flags_check = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = { var = GRE.debt@ENG value = 0 compare = less_than_or_equals }
            check_variable = { var = GRE.true_debt@ENG value = 0 compare = equals }
            NOT = { has_country_flag = GRE_debt_at_uk_fulfilled }
        }
        set_country_flag = GRE_debt_at_uk_fulfilled
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = { var = GRE.debt@FRA value = 0 compare = less_than_or_equals }
            check_variable = { var = GRE.true_debt@FRA value = 0 compare = equals }
            NOT = { has_country_flag = GRE_debt_at_fra_fulfilled }
        }
        set_country_flag = GRE_debt_at_fra_fulfilled
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = { var = GRE.debt@ITA value = 0 compare = less_than_or_equals }
            check_variable = { var = GRE.true_debt@ITA value = 0 compare = equals }
            NOT = { has_country_flag = GRE_debt_at_ita_fulfilled }
        }
        set_country_flag = GRE_debt_at_ita_fulfilled
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_country_flag = GRE_debt_at_uk_fulfilled
            has_country_flag = GRE_debt_at_fra_fulfilled
            has_country_flag = GRE_debt_at_ita_fulfilled
        }
        set_country_flag = GRE_debt_free
    }
}

####################################################################################
##############################[ Subsidized Factories ]##############################
####################################################################################

GRE_subsidized_check = {
    clear_variable = sub_civs 
    clear_variable = sub_mils 
    hidden_effect = {
        every_country = {
            limit = {
                is_in_array = {
                    array = global.favor_mechanic
                    value = THIS.id
                }
                has_opinion = { target = GRE value > 79 }  
                set_temp_variable = { chk = THIS.num_of_civilian_factories }
                add_to_temp_variable = { chk = THIS.num_of_military_factories }
                OR = { is_major = yes check_variable = { chk > 29 } has_country_flag=balkan_pact_reinforced }
                check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=30 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
            }
            if = { 
                limit = { has_country_flag = balkan_pact_reinforced }
                set_temp_variable = { c_civ_score = 0.050 }                                                                       # Score is 5.0% of country's civ factories.
                set_temp_variable = { c_mil_score = 0.050 }                                                                       # Score is 5.0% of country's mil factories.
            }
            else = {
                set_temp_variable = { c_civ_score = 0.015 }                                                                       # Score is 1.5% of country's civ factories.
                set_temp_variable = { c_mil_score = 0.015 }                                                                       # Score is 1.5% of country's mil factories.
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=30 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=40 compare=less_than }
                }
                if = { 
                    limit = { has_country_flag = balkan_pact_reinforced }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { c_civ_score = 0.006 }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { c_mil_score = 0.006 }
                }
                else = {
                    add_to_temp_variable = { c_civ_score = 0.003 }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { c_mil_score = 0.003 }
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=40 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=50 compare=less_than }
                }
                if = { 
                    limit = { has_country_flag = balkan_pact_reinforced }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { c_civ_score = 0.010 }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { c_mil_score = 0.010 }
                }
                else = {
                    add_to_temp_variable = { c_civ_score = 0.005 }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { c_mil_score = 0.005 }
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=50 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=60 compare=less_than }
                }
                if = { 
                    limit = { has_country_flag = balkan_pact_reinforced }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { c_civ_score = 0.014 }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { c_mil_score = 0.014 }
                }
                else = {
                    add_to_temp_variable = { c_civ_score = 0.007 }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { c_mil_score = 0.007 }
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=70 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=80 compare=less_than }
                }
                if = { 
                    limit = { has_country_flag = balkan_pact_reinforced }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { c_civ_score = 0.020 }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { c_mil_score = 0.020 }
                }
                else = {
                    add_to_temp_variable = { c_civ_score = 0.010 }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { c_mil_score = 0.010 }
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=80 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=90 compare=less_than }
                }
                if = { 
                    limit = { has_country_flag = balkan_pact_reinforced }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { c_civ_score = 0.030 }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { c_mil_score = 0.030 }
                }
                else = {
                    add_to_temp_variable = { c_civ_score = 0.015 }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { c_mil_score = 0.015 }
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=90 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=95 compare=less_than }
                }
                if = { 
                    limit = { has_country_flag = balkan_pact_reinforced }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { c_civ_score = 0.040 }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { c_mil_score = 0.040 }
                }
                else = {
                    add_to_temp_variable = { c_civ_score = 0.020 }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { c_mil_score = 0.020 }
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=95 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=100 compare=less_than_or_equals }
                }
                if = { 
                    limit = { has_country_flag = balkan_pact_reinforced }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { c_civ_score = 0.050 }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { c_mil_score = 0.050 }
                }
                else = {
                    add_to_temp_variable = { c_civ_score = 0.025 }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { c_mil_score = 0.025 }
                }
            }
            multiply_temp_variable = { c_civ_score = THIS.num_of_civilian_factories }                                         # BalPac: Minimum 5.6%, Maximum 10.0% of factories.
            multiply_temp_variable = { c_mil_score = THIS.num_of_military_factories }                                         # Normal: Minimum 1.8%, Maximum 4.0% of factories.
            add_to_temp_variable = { total_sub_civs = c_civ_score }
            add_to_temp_variable = { total_sub_mils = c_mil_score }
            log = "[THIS.GetNameDef]:   [?c_civ_score], [?c_mil_score] - [?THIS.num_of_civilian_factories], [?THIS.num_of_military_factories]"
        }
        round_temp_variable = total_sub_civs
        round_temp_variable = total_sub_mils
        GRE = {
            add_to_variable = { sub_civs = total_sub_civs }
            add_to_variable = { sub_mils = total_sub_mils }
        }
    }
}

####################################################################################
################################[ Bedrock Factories ]###############################

GRE_bedrock_check = {
    clear_variable =  bed_civs 
    hidden_effect = {
        every_country = {
            limit = {
                OR = { tag=TUR tag=BUL tag=YUG tag=ALB tag=ROM tag=HUN tag=CZE tag=AUS AND={ tag=GER AUS={ exists=no }}}
                exists=yes
                has_opinion = { target = GRE value > 79 }
                check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=30 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
            }
            if = { 
                limit = { has_country_flag = balkan_pact_reinforced }
                set_temp_variable = { inv_score = 0.150 }                                                                         # Score is 15.0% of country's civ factories.
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = balkan_pact_reinforced } }
                set_temp_variable = { inv_score = 0.100 }                                                                         # Score is 10.0% of country's civ factories.
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=30 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=40 compare=less_than }
                }
                if = { 
                    limit = { has_country_flag = balkan_pact_reinforced }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { inv_score = 0.020 }
                }
                else = {
                    add_to_temp_variable = { inv_score = 0.010 }
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=40 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=50 compare=less_than }
                }
                if = { 
                    limit = { has_country_flag = balkan_pact_reinforced }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { inv_score = 0.040 }
                }
                else = {
                    add_to_temp_variable = { inv_score = 0.020 }
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=50 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=60 compare=less_than }
                }
                if = { 
                    limit = { has_country_flag = balkan_pact_reinforced }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { inv_score = 0.060 }
                }
                else = {
                    add_to_temp_variable = { inv_score = 0.040 }
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=70 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=80 compare=less_than }
                }
                if = { 
                    limit = { has_country_flag = balkan_pact_reinforced }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { inv_score = 0.080 }
                }
                else = {
                    add_to_temp_variable = { inv_score = 0.060 }
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=80 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=90 compare=less_than }
                }
                if = { 
                    limit = { has_country_flag = balkan_pact_reinforced }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { inv_score = 0.100 }
                }
                else = {
                    add_to_temp_variable = { inv_score = 0.080 }
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=90 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=95 compare=less_than }
                }
                if = { 
                    limit = { has_country_flag = balkan_pact_reinforced }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { inv_score = 0.120 }
                }
                else = {
                    add_to_temp_variable = { inv_score = 0.100 }
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=95 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=100 compare=less_than_or_equals }
                }
                if = { 
                    limit = { has_country_flag = balkan_pact_reinforced }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { inv_score = 0.150 }
                }
                else = {
                    add_to_temp_variable = { inv_score = 0.120 }
                }
            }
            if = { limit={ tag=GER } divide_temp_variable={ inv_score=6 }}
            multiply_temp_variable = { inv_score = THIS.num_of_civilian_factories }                                         # BalPac: Minimum 17.0%, Maximum 30.0% of factories.                                       
            add_to_temp_variable = { total_bed_civs = inv_score }                                                           # Normal: Minimum 12.0%, Maximum 22.0% of factories.
            #log="Check This Out: [?inv_score] - [?THIS.num_of_civilian_factories]"
        }
        round_temp_variable = total_bed_civs
        GRE = { add_to_variable = { bed_civs = total_bed_civs }}
    }
}

#################################[ Mob.Economy Factories ]##############################

GRE_mobilized_check = {
    hidden_effect = {
        every_country = {
            limit = {
                is_in_array = {
                    array = global.favor_mechanic
                    value = THIS.id
                }
                has_opinion = { target = GRE value > 79 }  
                check_variable = { num_of_military_factories > 14 }
                check_variable = { var = favor@GRE value = 30 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            }
            if = { limit = { check_variable = { num_of_military_factories < 31 } } add_to_temp_variable = { x = 0.33 } }        # between 15-30
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { num_of_military_factories < 61 } } add_to_temp_variable = { x = 1 } }      # between 30-60
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { num_of_military_factories < 100 } } add_to_temp_variable = { x = 2 } }     # between 60-99
            else = { add_to_temp_variable = { x = 3 } }                                                                         # above 100+
            if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=30 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=40 compare=less_than }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { x = 0.20 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=40 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=50 compare=less_than }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { x = 0.33 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=50 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=60 compare=less_than }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { x = 0.50 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=70 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=80 compare=less_than }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { x = 0.75 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=80 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=90 compare=less_than }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { x = 1.00 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=90 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=95 compare=less_than }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { x = 1.50 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=95 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=favor@GRE value=100 compare=less_than_or_equals }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { x = 2.00 }
            }
        }
        round_temp_variable = x
        GRE = { set_variable = { mob_mils = x } } 
    }
}

GRE_budget_refresh = {

    clamp_variable = {
        var = GRE_budget_consumer
        min = 0
        max = 0.5
    }

    clamp_variable = {
        var = GRE_budget_construction
        min = -1
        max = 0
    }
    
    clamp_variable = {
        var = GRE_budget_pp_cost
        min = -2
        max = 0
    }
    
    clamp_variable = {
        var = GRE_budget_resources
        min = -1
        max = 0
    }
}

#############################################################################################
######################################[ WAR STRAIN EFFECTS ]#################################
#############################################################################################

GRE_update_strain_on_industry = {

    set_temp_variable = { x = max_available_manpower_k }                        #[0 manpower in field, -> +40% industry bonus] [ 250.000 manpower in field -> -30% industry bonus ] [ 1.500.000 manpower in field -> -80% industry bonus ]
    subtract_from_temp_variable = { x = manpower_k }
    add_to_temp_variable = { x = casualties_k } 
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = { x < 250 }
        }
        multiply_temp_variable = { x = -0.28 }                                 # y = 0.28x - 4
        add_to_temp_variable = { x = 40 }
    }
    else = {
        multiply_temp_variable = { x = -0.04 }                               # y = -0.04x - 20
        add_to_temp_variable = { x = -20 }
    }
    divide_temp_variable = { x = 100 }
    set_variable = { strain_fct = x }
    set_variable = { strain_dck = x }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = { grecoitalian_war_counter > 150 }
        }
        set_temp_variable = { x = grecoitalian_war_counter }
        divide_temp_variable = { x = -3000 }
        set_variable = { strain_atk = x }
        set_variable = { strain_def = x }
        set_variable = { strain_org = x }
    }
    else = {
        set_variable = { strain_atk = 0 }
        set_variable = { strain_def = 0 }
        set_variable = { strain_org = 0 }
    }
}

#############################################################################################
#######################################[ RETURN IC RATIO ]###################################
#############################################################################################

calculate_ticr_tmpT_THIS = {
    #scope: other country. Returns ticr (temp variable)
    if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { tmpT = 0 } }                         #Civ + Mil, Civ == Mil
        set_temp_variable = { ticr = GRE.num_of_factories }
        divide_temp_variable = { ticr = THIS.num_of_factories }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { tmpT = 1 } }                         #Civ + Mil, Mil = 2/3 Civ
        set_temp_variable = { ticr = GRE.num_of_military_factories }
        multiply_temp_variable = { ticr = 0.666 }
        add_to_temp_variable = { ticr = GRE.num_of_civilian_factories }
        set_temp_variable = { other_ticr = THIS.num_of_military_factories }
        multiply_temp_variable = { other_ticr = 0.666 }
        add_to_temp_variable = { other_ticr = THIS.num_of_civilian_factories }
        divide_temp_variable = { ticr = other_ticr }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { tmpT = 2 } }                         #Civ only
        set_temp_variable = { ticr = GRE.num_of_civilian_factories }
        divide_temp_variable = { ticr = THIS.num_of_civilian_factories }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { tmpT = 3 } }                         #Mil only
        set_temp_variable = { ticr = GRE.num_of_military_factories }
        divide_temp_variable = { ticr = THIS.num_of_military_factories }
    }
}
